I see exactly what was happening in the screenshot.\n\nThe selection bar (the tabs container) was using `sm:w-fit`, which tells the container to be exactly as wide as its content on desktop screens. Because you have a lot of tools (Crowd Prompt all the way through Slides), that \"fit\" width was wider than the actual panel it lived inside, causing it to clip right through the right edge and breaking the horizontal scroll.\n\n**The Fix:**\nI added `max-w-full` to the selection bar container. \n\nThis creates a perfect rule: The tab bar will now perfectly hug the buttons (`w-fit`), but it is strictly forbidden from growing wider than its parent panel (`max-w-full`).
